    "class NoDaemonProcess(multiprocessing.Process):\n",
    "    # make 'daemon' attribute always return False\n",
    "    def _get_daemon(self):\n",
    "        return False\n",
    "    def _set_daemon(self, value):\n",
    "        pass\n",
    "    daemon = property(_get_daemon, _set_daemon)\n",
    "\n",
    "class MyPool(multiprocessing.pool.Pool):\n",
    "    Process = NoDaemonProcess\n",
    "    \n",
    "def simplecount(filename):\n",
    "    lines = 0\n",
    "    for line in open(filename):\n",
    "        lines += 1\n",
    "    return lines\n",
    "\n",
    "# Function to be executed in parallel returning to the mapping function the sequence id the function gets as input in order\n",
    "# in order to know the mapping of the results on process \n",
    "def runParallelFunctionDebug(sequenceID):\n",
    "    classLabel1 = 'NData'\n",
    "    classLabel2 = 'BData'\n",
    "    classLabel3 = 'H'\n",
    "    classLabel4 = 'T'\n",
    "    thresholdClass1 = 90\n",
    "\n",
    "    indexFile = 0\n",
    "\n",
    "    print(matches[sequenceID])\n",
    "    return matches[sequenceID]\n",
    "\n",
    "# Function to be executed in parallel returning to the mapping function the sequence id the function gets as input in order\n",
    "# in order to know the mapping of the results on process \n",
    "def runParallelFunction(sequenceID):\n",
    "    classLabel1 = 'NData'\n",
    "    classLabel2 = 'BData'\n",
    "    classLabel3 = 'H'\n",
    "    classLabel4 = 'T'\n",
    "    thresholdClass1 = 90\n",
    "    \n",
    "    #global studyResults\n",
    "    global matches\n",
    "    \n",
    "    frameResults = pd.DataFrame([['PatientID',0,0, 0,0,0]],columns={'PatientID','FrameIDRow','FrameIDCol','Class1','Class2','Class3'})\n",
    "    frameResults['Class3'][0] = 0\n",
    "    frameResults['Class2'][0] = 0\n",
    "    frameResults['Class1'][0] = 0\n",
    "    \n",
    "    indexFile = sequenceID\n",
    "    framesIDs = matches[sequenceID]\n",
    "    \n",
    "    framesIDsTcell = framesIDs.replace(\"CELL_BALLOON_SNAPSHOT4\",\"CELL_NUC_SNAPSHOT4\")\n",
    "\n",
    "    #print framesIDs\n",
    "    with open(framesIDs) as data_file:    \n",
    "        data = json.load(data_file)\n",
    "        dataTcell = json.load(open(framesIDsTcell))\n",
    "\n",
    "        for fileID in (data['classifications']).keys():\n",
    "            fileIDParsed = fileID.split('/')\n",
    "            slideID = fileIDParsed[fileIDParsed.__len__()-3]\n",
    "            snapshotIDParsed = fileIDParsed[fileIDParsed.__len__()-1].split('_')\n",
    "            row = int(snapshotIDParsed[0])\n",
    "            col = int(snapshotIDParsed[1])\n",
    "            #print col\n",
    "            predictionCell = data['classifications'][fileID][0]\n",
    "            predictionTcell = dataTcell['classifications'][fileID.replace(\"CELL_BALLOON_SNAPSHOT4\",\"CELL_NUC_SNAPSHOT4\")][0]\n",
    "            #print predictionCell[1]\n",
    "\n",
    "            frameResults['PatientID'][0] = slideID\n",
    "            frameResults['FrameIDRow'][0] = row\n",
    "            frameResults['FrameIDCol'][0] = col\n",
    "\n",
    "            if((predictionCell[0]==classLabel2) & (predictionTcell[0]==classLabel3) & (predictionTcell[1]>=thresholdClass1) & (predictionCell[1]>=thresholdClass1)):\n",
    "                frameResults['Class2'][0] = frameResults['Class2'][0] + 1\n",
    "            else:\n",
    "                frameResults['Class1'][0] = frameResults['Class1'][0] + 1\n",
    "\n",
    "            if((predictionTcell[0]==classLabel4) & (predictionTcell[1]>=thresholdClass1)):\n",
    "                frameResults['Class3'][0] = frameResults['Class3'][0] + 1\n",
    "\n",
    "            #print frameResults['Class2']\n",
    "    #studyResultsTmp = [studyResults,frameResults]\n",
    "    #studyResults = pd.concat(studyResultsTmp)\n",
    "\n",
    "        \n",
    "    return frameResults\n",
    "\n",
    "def separateStains(rawImageRGB,deconvMatrix):\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Create an artificial color close to the orginal one\n",
    "    ihc_hdx = separate_stains(rawImageRGB, deconvMatrix)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    return(ihc_hdx)"

    "def parallelSlideAnalysis(sequenceID):\n",
    "    \n",
    "    global matches\n",
    "    global studyHistodistribution \n",
    "    global nmbBins \n",
    "    \n",
    "    distributionHistochanels = np.zeros([1,nmbBins*2+4])\n",
    "    \n",
    "    #print (matches[sequenceID])\n",
    "    img  = OpenSlide(matches[sequenceID])\n",
    "    \n",
    "    img_dimensions = (img.dimensions)        # Retourne la dimension global \n",
    "    #print(img.properties)        # Un tas de mÃ©tadata \n",
    "    img_level_count = (img.level_count)       # Retourne le nombre dâ€™Ã©tage dans la pyramide \n",
    "    img_level_dimensions = (img.level_dimensions)  # Retourne les dimensions de chaque Ã©tages\n",
    "    img_level_downsamples = (img.level_downsamples) # Retourne le zoom de chaque Ã©tages\n",
    "\n",
    "    #lowres = img.read_region(location=(10,10), level=6, size=img_level_dimensions[5])\n",
    "    #lowres = img.read_region(location=(200,200), level=6, size=img_level_dimensions[7])\n",
    "    lowres = img.get_thumbnail((5000,10000))\n",
    "\n",
    "    arr = array(lowres)\n",
    "    arr.shape\n",
    "    \n",
    "    arrDeconv = separate_stains(arr[:,:,0:3],fgx_from_rgb)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    # first channel statistics\n",
    "    \n",
    "    vecPixval = arrDeconv[:,:,0].flatten()*1.0\n",
    "    vecPixvalNorm = (vecPixval - np.percentile(vecPixval,5))/np.abs(np.percentile(vecPixval,95)-np.percentile(vecPixval,5))*255\n",
    "    vecPixvalNorm[np.where(vecPixvalNorm<=0)[0]]=0\n",
    "    vecPixvalNorm[np.where(vecPixval>=255)[0]]=255\n",
    "    foregroundPix = np.where((vecPixvalNorm>0)&(vecPixvalNorm<255))[0]\n",
    "    resHistVal = np.histogram(vecPixvalNorm[foregroundPix],bins=range(0,255,2),normed=True)\n",
    "    distributionHistochanels[0,:127] = resHistVal[0]\n",
    "    distributionHistochanels[0,127] = np.percentile(vecPixval,5)\n",
    "    distributionHistochanels[0,128] = np.percentile(vecPixval,95)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # second channel statistics\n",
    "    \n",
    "    vecPixval = arrDeconv[:,:,1].flatten()*1.0\n",
    "    vecPixvalNorm = (vecPixval - np.percentile(vecPixval,5))/np.abs(np.percentile(vecPixval,95)-np.percentile(vecPixval,5))*255\n",
    "    vecPixvalNorm[np.where(vecPixvalNorm<=0)[0]]=0\n",
    "    vecPixvalNorm[np.where(vecPixval>=255)[0]]=255\n",
    "    foregroundPix = np.where((vecPixvalNorm>0)&(vecPixvalNorm<255))[0]\n",
    "    resHistVal = np.histogram(vecPixvalNorm[foregroundPix],bins=range(0,255,2),normed=True)\n",
    "    distributionHistochanels[0,129:256] = resHistVal[0]\n",
    "    distributionHistochanels[0,256] = np.percentile(vecPixval,5)\n",
    "    distributionHistochanels[0,257] = np.percentile(vecPixval,95)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    studyHistodistribution[sequenceID,:] = distributionHistochanels\n",
    "    \n",
    "    #print(resHistVal[0])\n",
    "    \n",
    "    return(distributionHistochanels)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def parallelSlideFOVAnalysis(sequenceID):\n",
    "    import skimage.io as io\n",
    "    from skimage.color import rgb2gray\n",
    "    global matchesDB127str\n",
    "    \n",
    "    slideFname = str(matchesDB127str[sequenceID])\n",
    "    slideFnameParse = slideFname.split(\"/\")\n",
    "    slideIDstr = str(slideFnameParse[6]).replace(\".mrxs\",\"\")\n",
    "    slideDecompDir = \"/home/erexhepa/PRODUCTION_GFT505_PRECLINICAL/VALIDATION/\"+slideIDstr+\"_files\"   \n",
    "    slideDecompFname = \"/home/erexhepa/PRODUCTION_GFT505_PRECLINICAL/VALIDATION/\"+slideIDstr+\"_PS_files_LIST4XFOV.txt\"\n",
    "    \n",
    "    def SubDirPath (d):\n",
    "        return filter(os.path.isdir, [os.path.join(d,f) for f in os.listdir(d)])\n",
    "    \n",
    "    if(os.path.exists(slideDecompDir)):\n",
    "        \n",
    "        listSlideSubdir = SubDirPath(slideDecompDir)\n",
    "\n",
    "        slideDecompDir = slideDecompDir + \"/14\"\n",
    "\n",
    "        matchesFOVs= []\n",
    "\n",
    "        framelistFile = open(slideDecompFname,\"w\")\n",
    "\n",
    "        for file in glob.glob(slideDecompDir+\"/*.jpeg\"):\n",
    "            slidepathIterative  = (os.path.join(slideDecompDir,file))\n",
    "            matchesFOVs.append(slidepathIterative)\n",
    "\n",
    "        for fovsIds in range(matchesFOVs.__len__()):\n",
    "            try:\n",
    "                fileIDIt = str(matchesFOVs[fovsIds])\n",
    "                fovIM = io.imread(fileIDIt)\n",
    "\n",
    "                arr = array(fovIM)\n",
    "                arrDeconv = separate_stains(arr[:,:,0:3],fgx_from_rgb)\n",
    "\n",
    "                normMin = np.min(arrDeconv[:,:,0].flatten())\n",
    "                normMax = np.max(arrDeconv[:,:,0].flatten())\n",
    "\n",
    "                foregroundData = (arrDeconv[:,:,0]-normMin)/(normMax-normMin)\n",
    "\n",
    "                fovIMgray = rgb2gray(fovIM)\n",
    "                fgPrcnt = ((np.where(fovIMgray<0.9)[0].flatten()).__len__()*100.0/(fovIM.shape[0]*fovIM.shape[1]))\n",
    "\n",
    "                if((fgPrcnt>=0)):\n",
    "                    outputfovstr = fileIDIt + \",%f\" % fgPrcnt \n",
    "                    outputfovstr = outputfovstr + \",%d\" % int(matchesDB124.FibrosisScoreCat.iloc[sequenceID])\n",
    "                    framelistFile.write(\"%s\\n\" % outputfovstr)\n",
    "            except:\n",
    "                print(\"catched error\")\n",
    "                \n",
    "        framelistFile.close()\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "        \n",
    "def parallelSlideFOVAnalysisStats(sequenceID):\n",
    "    import skimage.io as io\n",
    "    from skimage.color import rgb2gray\n",
    "    global matchesFOVs\n",
    "    from PIL import Image\n",
    "    import math\n",
    "    import random\n",
    "    from PIL import Image\n",
    "    \n",
    "    slideFname = str(matchesFOVs.iloc[sequenceID])\n",
    "    slideFnameParse = slideFname.split(\"/\")\n",
    "    slideDecompFname = \"/home/erexhepa/PRODUCTION_GFT505_PRECLINICAL/FOV_List_stats_LIST4XFOV_levyc_red.txt\"\n",
    "    framelistFile = open(slideDecompFname,\"a+\")\n",
    "\n",
    "    #if(1):\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "            fileIDIt = str(str(matchesFOVs.iloc[sequenceID]))\n",
    "            \n",
    "            fovIM = io.imread(fileIDIt)\n",
    "\n",
    "            arr = array(fovIM)\n",
    "            arrDeconv = separate_stains(arr[:,:,0:3],fgx_from_rgb)\n",
    "\n",
    "            normMin = np.min(arrDeconv[:,:,0].flatten())\n",
    "            normMax = np.max(arrDeconv[:,:,0].flatten())\n",
    "\n",
    "            foregroundData = (arrDeconv[:,:,0]-normMin)/(normMax-normMin)\n",
    "\n",
    "            fovIMgray = rgb2gray(fovIM)\n",
    "            fgPrcnt    = ((np.where(fovIMgray<0.9)[0].flatten()).__len__()*100.0/(fovIM.shape[0]*fovIM.shape[1]))\n",
    "            fgFibPrcnt = ((np.where(foregroundData>0.4)[0].flatten()).__len__()*100.0/(fovIM.shape[0]*fovIM.shape[1]))\n",
    "            \n",
    "            # compute fractal dimension\n",
    "            imgx = fovIMgray.shape[0]\n",
    "            imgy = fovIMgray.shape[1] # will be auto-re-adjusted according to aspect ratio of the fractal\n",
    "            maxIt = imgx * imgy * 2\n",
    "    \n",
    "            fractalName = \"Barnsley Fern\"\n",
    "            mat=[[0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.16, 0.0, 0.0, 0.01],\n",
    "                 [0.85, 0.04, -0.04, 0.85, 0.0, 1.6, 0.85],\n",
    "                 [0.2, -0.26, 0.23, 0.22, 0.0, 1.6, 0.07],\n",
    "                 [-0.15, 0.28, 0.26, 0.24, 0.0, 0.44, 0.07]]\n",
    "            \n",
    "            fractalName = \"Levy C curve\"\n",
    "            mat = [[0.5, -0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.0, 0.0, 0.5],\n",
    "                   [0.5, 0.5, -0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5]]\n",
    "                        fractalName = \"Dragon curve\"\n",
    "            \n",
    "            mat = [[0.5, -0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.0, 0.0, 0.5],\n",
    "                   [-0.5, -0.5, 0.5, -0.5, 1.0, 0.0, 0.5]]\n",
    "            \n",
    "            m = len(mat) # number of IFS transformations\n",
    "            \n",
    "            # find xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax of the fractal using IFS algorithm\n",
    "            x = mat[0][4]\n",
    "            y = mat[0][5] \n",
    "            xa = x\n",
    "            xb = x\n",
    "            ya = y\n",
    "            yb = y\n",
    "            \n",
    "            for k in range(maxIt):\n",
    "                i = random.randint(0, m - 1)\n",
    "                if random.random() <= mat[i][6]:\n",
    "                    x0 = x * mat[i][0] + y * mat[i][1] + mat[i][4] \n",
    "                    y  = x * mat[i][2] + y * mat[i][3] + mat[i][5] \n",
    "                    x = x0 \n",
    "                    if x < xa:\n",
    "                        xa = x\n",
    "                    if x > xb:\n",
    "                        xb = x\n",
    "                    if y < ya:\n",
    "                        ya = y\n",
    "                    if y > yb:\n",
    "                        yb = y\n",
    "            \n",
    "           \n",
    "            impilFovIMgray = Image.fromarray(np.uint8((foregroundData)*255))\n",
    "            image = impilFovIMgray\n",
    "            \n",
    "                \n",
    "            pixels = image.load()\n",
    "            \n",
    "            #print(\"test\")\n",
    "            \n",
    "            theColor = (0.4*255)\n",
    "            \n",
    "            \n",
    "            \n",
    "            b = 2 # initial box size in pixels\n",
    "            f = 2 # box scaling factor\n",
    "            n = 3 # number of graph points for simple linear regression\n",
    "            gx = [] # x coordinates of graph points\n",
    "            gy = [] # y coordinates of graph points\n",
    "            for ib in range(n):\n",
    "                bs = b * f ** ib # box size in pixels\n",
    "                bnx = int(imgx / bs) # of boxes in x direction of image\n",
    "                bny = int(imgy / bs) # of boxes in y direction of image\n",
    "                boxCount = 0\n",
    "                for by in range(bny):\n",
    "                    for bx in range(bnx):\n",
    "                        # if there are any pixels in the box then increase box count\n",
    "                        foundPixel = False\n",
    "                        for ky in range(bs):\n",
    "                            for kx in range(bs):\n",
    "                                if pixels[bs * bx + kx, bs * by + ky] >= theColor:\n",
    "                                    foundPixel = True\n",
    "                                    boxCount += 1\n",
    "                                    break\n",
    "                            if foundPixel:\n",
    "                                break\n",
    "                if(boxCount>0):\n",
    "                    gx.append(math.log(1.0 / bs))\n",
    "                    gy.append(math.log(boxCount)) \n",
    "\n",
    "            if(gx.__len__()>2):\n",
    "                # simple linear regression\n",
    "                x_ = 0.0\n",
    "                y_ = 0.0\n",
    "                x2_ = 0.0\n",
    "                xy_ = 0.0\n",
    "                for j in range(n):\n",
    "                    x_ += gx[j]\n",
    "                    y_ += gy[j]\n",
    "                    x2_ += gx[j] ** 2\n",
    "                    xy_ += gx[j] * gy[j]\n",
    "                x_ = x_ / n\n",
    "                y_ = y_ / n\n",
    "                x2_ = x2_ / n\n",
    "                xy_ = xy_ / n\n",
    "                b = (xy_ - x_ * y_) / (x2_ - x_ ** 2) # slope of the regression line\n",
    "            else:\n",
    "                b=0\n",
    "                \n",
    "            \n",
    "            if((fgPrcnt>=0)):\n",
    "                outputfovstr = fileIDIt + \",%f\" % fgPrcnt \n",
    "                outputfovstr = outputfovstr + \",%d\" % int(sequenceID)\n",
    "                outputfovstr = outputfovstr + \",%f\" % fgFibPrcnt \n",
    "                outputfovstr = outputfovstr + \",%f\" % b\n",
    "                framelistFile.write(\"%s\\n\" % outputfovstr)\n",
    "    except:\n",
    "            outputfovstr = fileIDIt + \",%f\" % 0 \n",
    "            outputfovstr = outputfovstr + \",%d\" % int(sequenceID)\n",
    "            outputfovstr = outputfovstr + \",%f\" % 0 \n",
    "            outputfovstr = outputfovstr + \",%f\" % 0\n",
    "            framelistFile.write(\"%s\\n\" % outputfovstr)\n",
    "                \n",
    "    framelistFile.close()"
   ]
  },
